<script type="text/javascript">
var isIE=(document.all)?1:0;

function refresh()
{
	window.location.reload(true);
}

function validateForm()
{
	var date = document.getElementById("date").value;
	if(date == "select")
	{
		alert("Please select Expiry date");
		return false;
	}
	else
	{
		return true;
	}
}

function goBtnClick(strSymbol)
{

	//alert(strSymbol);
	if(strSymbol == "index")
	{	
		var sym = document.ocForm.symbol.value = $("#optnContract").val();
		if(sym == "select")
		{
			alert("Please select underlying Indices");
			
			return false;
		}		
		else
		{	
			if (sym.indexOf('%26')>=0){
					location.href = '/marketinfo/sym_map/symbolMapping.jsp?symbol='+sym+'&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17';
				}
				else{
			//alert('/marketinfo/sym_map/symbolMapping.jsp?symbol='+sym+'&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17');
				//location.href = '/marketinfo/sym_map/symbolMapping.jsp?symbol='+escape(sym)+'&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17';
				
				
				if(sym == "NIFTY")
				{
				location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10003&symbol=NIFTY&symbol=NIFTY&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				
				if(sym == "NIFTYINFRA")
				{
				location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10004&symbol=NIFTYINFRA&symbol=NIFTYINFRA&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				
				if(sym == "NIFTYIT")
				{
				location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10005&symbol=NIFTYIT&symbol=NIFTYIT&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				
				if(sym == "NIFTYPSE")
				{
				location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10007&symbol=NIFTYPSE&symbol=NIFTYPSE&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				
				if(sym == "BANKNIFTY")
				{
					location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-9999&symbol=BANKNIFTY&symbol=BANKNIFTY&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}


				if(sym == "NIFTYMID50")
				{
				location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10006&symbol=NIFTYMID50&symbol=NIFTYMID50&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}
				
				if(sym == "S&P500")
				{
					location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10008&symbol=S%26P500&symbol=S%26P500&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				
				if(sym == "FTSE100")
				{
					location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10001&symbol=FTSE100&symbol=FTSE100&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				if(sym == "NIFTYCPSE")
				{
					location.href='/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbolCode=-10004&symbol=NIFTYCPSE&symbol=NIFTYCPSE&instrument=OPTIDX&date=-&segmentLink=17&segmentLink=17';
				}

				}
				
		}	
	}
	if(strSymbol == "stock")
	{	
		var sym = $("#underlyStock").val();
		sym = trimSpaces(sym);
		if(sym=="Search for an underlying stock:")
		{
			alert("Please Enter underlying stock");
		}
		else	
		{
			if(sym.length<2)
			{
				alert("Please enter more than 2 character in underlying stock");
			}
			else
			{	
				var instru = document.ocForm.instrument.value;
					location.href = '/marketinfo/sym_map/symbolMapping.jsp?symbol='+escape(sym)+'&instrument=OPTSTK&date=-&segmentLink=17';
			}	
		}
	}
}
//capEvents();
function popup ( url ) {
    chartpopup = window.open( url,'chartspopup','location=no,menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=no,status=yes,width=780,height=500,scrollbars=yes,screenX=0,screenY=0,left=0,top=0');
    chartpopup.focus();
}
function chartPopup(symbl, instrumen, dat, strke, calOrput, mainSymbol ){
	var dFormat = "ddNNNyyyy";
		var startDate = new Date(getDateFromFormat(dat,dFormat));
		var tameDate = formatDate(startDate,'dd-MM-yyyy');
	var url="/charts/webtame/webchart.jsp?OISymbol="+escape(mainSymbol)+"&CDSymbol="+escape(symbl)+"&Segment=FO&Instrument="+instrumen+"&Series=EQ&CDExpiryMonth=&FOExpiryMonth="+tameDate+"&IRFExpiryMonth=&CDDate1=&CDDate2=&PeriodType=2&Periodicity=1&StrikePrice="+strke+"&OptionType="+calOrput+"&Template=fo_options_Intrday.jsp";
	popup ( url );
	
}

function popup1 ( symbl,instrumen,dat,strke,calOrput ) {
	symbl=encodeURIComponent(symbl);
	instrumen=encodeURIComponent(instrumen);
	dat=encodeURIComponent(dat);
	strke=encodeURIComponent(strke);
	calOrput=encodeURIComponent(calOrput);
    url="/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/get_quote/GetQuoteFO.jsp?underlying="+symbl+"&instrument="+instrumen+"&expiry="+dat+"&type="+calOrput+"&strike="+strke
    printpopup = window.open( url,'printpopup','location=no,menubar=yes,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,status=yes,maximizable=true,screenX=0,screenY=0,left=0,top=0');printpopup.focus();
    //location.href = url;
}
function submitRequest(symbol,instrument)
{
	var date = document.optionChain.expirydate.options[document.optionChain.expirydate.selectedIndex].value;
	//alert(date);
	//location.href = '/marketinfo/fo/optionKeys.jsp?symbol='+symbol+'&instrument='+instrument+'&date='+date;
	location.href = '/live_market/dynaContent/live_watch/option_chain/optionKeys.jsp?symbol='+symbol+'&instrument='+instrument+'&date='+date;
}
